## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 1024
IN_FEATURES = 8192
OUT_FEATURES = 8192
NUM_GROUPS = 16
GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
HARDTANH_MIN = -2.0
HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
EPS = 1e-05

WARP_SIZE = 64
NUM_WARPS = 4
BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
WARP_M = 32
WARP_N = 32
K_TILE = 16

A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N

A_PACK_ELEMS = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8
B_PACK_ELEMS = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8
A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_ELEMS * 2
B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_ELEMS * 2


def _launch_gemm():
    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))


def _launch_post():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_kernel(
    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_ELEMS,), S.bf16),
    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_ELEMS,), S.bf16),
    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)

        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)

        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

        for frag_half in S.range(2):
            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]

        S.syncthreads()

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)

        S.syncthreads()

    lane_col = lane % 32
    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)


@substrate.jit
def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
):
    for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for group in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                mean += S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32)
            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                diff = S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
                var += diff * diff
            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                value = (S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
                value = value * S.convert(gn_weight[c], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c], S.f32)
                if value < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
                    value = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
                if value > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
                    value = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
                y[row, c] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)


def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
    first = xb[:, :, :, 0:8]
    second = xb[:, :, :, 8:16]
    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()


def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
    groups = []
    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=-1))
    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
        super().__init__()
        self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
        self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
        self._cached_weight_ptr = None
        self._cached_bias_ptr = None
        self._cached_gn_weight_ptr = None
        self._cached_gn_bias_ptr = None
        self._b_pack = None
        self._bias = None
        self._gn_weight = None
        self._gn_bias = None
        self._y = None

    def _refresh_static_buffers(self, device, dtype):
        w = self.gemm.weight
        b = self.gemm.bias
        gw = self.group_norm.weight
        gb = self.group_norm.bias

        w_ptr = w.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        b_ptr = b.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        gw_ptr = gw.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        gb_ptr = gb.untyped_storage().data_ptr()

        if (
            self._b_pack is None
            or self._cached_weight_ptr != w_ptr
            or self._b_pack.device != device
            or self._b_pack.dtype != dtype
        ):
            w_t = w.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._b_pack = _pack_b(w_t)
            self._cached_weight_ptr = w_ptr

        if (
            self._bias is None
            or self._cached_bias_ptr != b_ptr
            or self._bias.device != device
            or self._bias.dtype != dtype
        ):
            self._bias = b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_bias_ptr = b_ptr

        if (
            self._gn_weight is None
            or self._cached_gn_weight_ptr != gw_ptr
            or self._gn_weight.device != device
            or self._gn_weight.dtype != dtype
        ):
            self._gn_weight = gw.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_gn_weight_ptr = gw_ptr

        if (
            self._gn_bias is None
            or self._cached_gn_bias_ptr != gb_ptr
            or self._gn_bias.device != device
            or self._gn_bias.dtype != dtype
        ):
            self._gn_bias = gb.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_gn_bias_ptr = gb_ptr

        if self._y is None or self._y.device != device or self._y.dtype != dtype:
            self._y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=device, dtype=dtype)

    def forward(self, x):
        if (
            tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES)
            or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16
            or self.group_norm.num_groups != NUM_GROUPS
            or self.hardtanh.min_val != HARDTANH_MIN
            or self.hardtanh.max_val != HARDTANH_MAX
            or self.group_norm.eps != EPS
        ):
            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")

        x_contig = x.contiguous()
        self._refresh_static_buffers(x_contig.device, x_contig.dtype)
        a_pack = _pack_a(x_contig)
        gemm_mfma_kernel[_launch_gemm](a_pack.view(-1), self._b_pack.view(-1), self._bias, self._y)
        groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel[_launch_post](self._y, self._gn_weight, self._gn_bias)
        return self._y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

import substrate
import substrate.language as S

NUM_GROUPS = 16

        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)

        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)

        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

        for frag_half in S.range(2):
            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]

        S.syncthreads()

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)

        S.syncthreads()

    lane_col = lane % 32
    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)


@substrate.jit
def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
):
    for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for group in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                mean += S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32)
            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                diff = S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
                var += diff * diff
            var = var / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            denom = S.sqrt(var + S.convert(EPS, S.f32))
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                value = (S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32) - mean) / denom
                value = value * S.convert(gn_weight[c], S.f32) + S.convert(gn_bias[c], S.f32)
                if value < S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32):
                    value = S.convert(HARDTANH_MIN, S.f32)
                if value > S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32):
                    value = S.convert(HARDTANH_MAX, S.f32)
                y[row, c] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)


def _pack_a(x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
    first = xb[:, :, :, 0:8]
    second = xb[:, :, :, 8:16]
    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()


def _pack_b(w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
    groups = []
    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=-1))
    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
        super().__init__()
        self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
        self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)
        self._cached_weight_ptr = None
        self._cached_bias_ptr = None
        self._cached_gn_weight_ptr = None
        self._cached_gn_bias_ptr = None
        self._b_pack = None
        self._bias = None
        self._gn_weight = None
        self._gn_bias = None
        self._y = None

    def _refresh_static_buffers(self, device, dtype):
        w = self.gemm.weight
        b = self.gemm.bias
        gw = self.group_norm.weight
        gb = self.group_norm.bias

        w_ptr = w.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        b_ptr = b.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        gw_ptr = gw.untyped_storage().data_ptr()
        gb_ptr = gb.untyped_storage().data_ptr()

        if (
            self._b_pack is None
            or self._cached_weight_ptr != w_ptr
            or self._b_pack.device != device
            or self._b_pack.dtype != dtype
        ):
            w_t = w.t().to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._b_pack = _pack_b(w_t)
            self._cached_weight_ptr = w_ptr

        if (
            self._bias is None
            or self._cached_bias_ptr != b_ptr
            or self._bias.device != device
            or self._bias.dtype != dtype
        ):
            self._bias = b.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_bias_ptr = b_ptr

        if (
            self._gn_weight is None
            or self._cached_gn_weight_ptr != gw_ptr
            or self._gn_weight.device != device
            or self._gn_weight.dtype != dtype
        ):
            self._gn_weight = gw.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_gn_weight_ptr = gw_ptr

        if (
            self._gn_bias is None
            or self._cached_gn_bias_ptr != gb_ptr
            or self._gn_bias.device != device
            or self._gn_bias.dtype != dtype
        ):
            self._gn_bias = gb.to(device=device, dtype=dtype).contiguous()
            self._cached_gn_bias_ptr = gb_ptr

        if self._y is None or self._y.device != device or self._y.dtype != dtype:
            self._y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), device=device, dtype=dtype)

    def forward(self, x):
        if (
            tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES)
            or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16
            or self.group_norm.num_groups != NUM_GROUPS
            or self.hardtanh.min_val != HARDTANH_MIN
            or self.hardtanh.max_val != HARDTANH_MAX
            or self.group_norm.eps != EPS
        ):
            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")

        x_contig = x.contiguous()
        self._refresh_static_buffers(x_contig.device, x_contig.dtype)
        a_pack = _pack_a(x_contig)
        gemm_mfma_kernel[_launch_gemm](a_pack.view(-1), self._b_pack.view(-1), self._bias, self._y)
        groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel[_launch_post](self._y, self._gn_weight, self._gn_bias)
        return self._y

codex
I’m replacing the simple `for k_tile` loop with a double-buffered pairwise pipeline now: preload two K-tiles into LDS, consume them via two natural MFMA steps each, and refill the consumed buffer with the next tile before it is needed again.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn

class Model(nn.Module):
    """
    Simple model that performs a GEMM, applies Group Normalization, and then HardTanh.
    """
    def __init__(self, in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max):
        super(Model, self).__init__()
        self.gemm = nn.Linear(in_features, out_features)
        self.group_norm = nn.GroupNorm(num_groups, out_features)
        self.hardtanh = nn.Hardtanh(min_val=hardtanh_min, max_val=hardtanh_max)

    def forward(self, x):
        """
        Args:
            x (torch.Tensor): Input tensor of shape (batch_size, in_features).
        Returns:
            torch.Tensor: Output tensor of shape (batch_size, out_features).
        """
        x = self.gemm(x)
        x = self.group_norm(x)
        x = self.hardtanh(x)
        return x

batch_size = 1024
in_features = 8192
out_features = 8192
num_groups = 16
hardtanh_min = -2.0
hardtanh_max = 2.0

def get_inputs():
    return [torch.rand(batch_size, in_features, dtype=torch.bfloat16)]

def get_init_inputs():
    return [in_features, out_features, num_groups, hardtanh_min, hardtanh_max]

## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.
  
MFMA swizzle invariants:
  For A, `i in [0,32)`, `j in [0,8)`: `A(i, j) -> (lane_id = i + (j / 4) * 32, element = j % 4)`
  For B, `j in [0,8)`, `i in [0,32)`: `B(j, i) -> (lane_id = j + (i / 4) * 32, element = i % 4)`

Accumulator invariant for C: for each lane in [0, 64) and acc_idx in [0, 16):
  - col = tile_col_base + (lane % 32)
  - row = tile_row_base + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * (lane // 32) + (acc_idx % 4)

Do not invent a different unpacking. Do not use a naive acc_idx -> contiguous row mapping. Treat this mapping as fixed when writing results.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 1024
IN_FEATURES = 8192
OUT_FEATURES = 8192
NUM_GROUPS = 16
GROUP_SIZE = OUT_FEATURES // NUM_GROUPS
HARDTANH_MIN = -2.0
HARDTANH_MAX = 2.0
EPS = 1e-05

WARP_SIZE = 64
NUM_WARPS = 4
BLOCK_THREADS = WARP_SIZE * NUM_WARPS
BLOCK_M = 64
BLOCK_N = 64
WARP_M = 32
WARP_N = 32
K_TILE = 16

A_PACK_M = BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M
A_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
B_PACK_K = IN_FEATURES // K_TILE
B_PACK_N = OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N

A_PACK_ELEMS = A_PACK_M * A_PACK_K * WARP_SIZE * 8
B_PACK_ELEMS = B_PACK_K * B_PACK_N * WARP_SIZE * 8
A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = A_PACK_ELEMS * 2
B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES = B_PACK_ELEMS * 2


def _launch_gemm():
    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))


def _launch_post():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_kernel(
    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_ELEMS,), S.bf16),
    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_ELEMS,), S.bf16),
    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.bf16),
    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)

    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)

        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)

        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

codex
I’m checking the pack/unpack math outside the harness with a tiny standalone script. If the current swizzle logic is wrong, that will show up immediately and is faster than blind kernel edits.
exec
/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import torch

WARP_M=32; WARP_N=32; K_TILE=16; WARP_SIZE=64

def pack_a(x):
    BATCH_SIZE, IN_FEATURES = x.shape
    xb = x.view(BATCH_SIZE // WARP_M, WARP_M, IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
    first = xb[:, :, :, 0:8]
    second = xb[:, :, :, 8:16]
    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()

def pack_b(w):
    IN_FEATURES, OUT_FEATURES = w.shape
    wb = w.view(IN_FEATURES // K_TILE, K_TILE, OUT_FEATURES // WARP_N, WARP_N).permute(0, 2, 1, 3)
    groups = []
    for g in range(WARP_N // 4):
        cols = wb[:, :, :, g * 4 : (g + 1) * 4]
        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:, :, 0:8, :], cols[:, :, 8:16, :]), dim=-1))
    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()

B=64; K=16; N=32
x = torch.arange(B*K, dtype=torch.float32).reshape(B,K)
w = torch.arange(K*N, dtype=torch.float32).reshape(K,N)
pa = pack_a(x).view(2,64,8)
pb = pack_b(w).view(1,64,8)
acc = torch.zeros((64,16), dtype=torch.float32)
# emulate candidate mfma mapping assumptions: each lane has 8 bf16 => two halves of 4 values.
# A mapping from lane/elem/half to matrix indices from pack_a layout:
# For half h, lane<32 row=lane else row=lane-32, k=4*h + elem + (8 if lane>=32 else 0)?
# We'll directly decode from original x and w based on pack layout.
# candidate writeback mapping
for lane in range(64):
    for acc_idx in range(16):
        col = lane % 32
        row = 8*(acc_idx//4) + 4*(lane//32) + (acc_idx%4)
        # brute force dot for that output
        acc[lane,acc_idx] = (x[row] * w[:,col]).sum()

# compare with normal gemm tile flattened by mapping
ref = x @ w
maxdiff=0
for lane in range(64):
    for acc_idx in range(16):
        col = lane % 32
        row = 8*(acc_idx//4) + 4*(lane//32) + (acc_idx%4)
        maxdiff=max(maxdiff, abs(acc[lane,acc_idx]-ref[row,col]).item())
print('mapping maxdiff', maxdiff)
print('pa lane0', pa[0,0], pa[1,0])
print('pb lane0', pb[0,0])
print('pb lane8', pb[0,8])
print('pb lane32', pb[0,32])

codex
The GEMM/layout math is internally consistent enough that the next concrete suspect is parameter precision. I’m switching the bias and GroupNorm affine parameters to cached `f32` buffers so the fused epilogue matches PyTorch more closely while keeping the MFMA path in bf16.

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch, json, os
round_dir='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds/round2'

def load(path,name):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name,path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod
inp=load(f'{round_dir}/input_model.py','inp')
out=load(f'{round_dir}/output_model_new.py','out')

torch.manual_seed(0)
ref=inp.Model(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to('cuda')
torch.manual_seed(0)
mod=out.ModelNew(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to('cuda')
mod.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict())
x=inp.get_inputs()[0].to('cuda')
with torch.no_grad():
    y_ref=ref(x)
    y=mod(x)
    d=(y.float()-y_ref.float()).abs()
    print('final max', d.max().item(), 'mean', d.mean().item())
    # compare gemm only
    x_contig=x.contiguous()
    mod._refresh_static_buffers(x_contig.device, x_contig.dtype)
    a_pack=out._pack_a(x_contig)
    out.gemm_mfma_kernel[out._launch_gemm()](a_pack.view(-1), mod._b_pack.view(-1), mod._bias, mod._y)
    y_gemm=mod._y.clone()
    y_ref_gemm=ref.gemm(x)
    dg=(y_gemm.float()-y_ref_gemm.float()).abs()
    print('gemm max', dg.max().item(), 'mean', dg.mean().item())
PY" in /workspace/kernel_benchmark

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch
round_dir='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds/round2'

def load(path,name):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name,path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod
inp=load(f'{round_dir}/input_model.py','inp')
out=load(f'{round_dir}/output_model_new.py','out')

torch.manual_seed(0)
ref=inp.Model(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to(device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
torch.manual_seed(0)
mod=out.ModelNew(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to(device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
mod.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict())
x=inp.get_inputs()[0].to('cuda')
with torch.no_grad():
    y_ref=ref(x)
    y=mod(x)
    d=(y.float()-y_ref.float()).abs()
    print('final max', d.max().item(), 'mean', d.mean().item())
    x_contig=x.contiguous()
    mod._refresh_static_buffers(x_contig.device, x_contig.dtype)
    a_pack=out._pack_a(x_contig)
    out.gemm_mfma_kernel[out._launch_gemm()](a_pack.view(-1), mod._b_pack.view(-1), mod._bias, mod._y)
    y_gemm=mod._y.clone()
    y_ref_gemm=ref.gemm(x)
    dg=(y_gemm.float()-y_ref_gemm.float()).abs()
    print('gemm max', dg.max().item(), 'mean', dg.mean().item())
PY" in /workspace/kernel_benchmark

codex
I found a concrete swizzle bug: `A` is packed with the wrong 8-element lane ordering for the two natural MFMA steps. I’m fixing `_pack_a` to interleave the K subfragments as `[0:4, 8:12]` and `[4:8, 12:16]`, which matches the 32-lane / 32-lane A invariant across the two MFMA halves.
apply patch

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch
round_dir='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds/round2'

def load(path,name):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name,path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod
inp=load(f'{round_dir}/input_model.py','inp')
out=load(f'{round_dir}/output_model_new.py','out')

torch.manual_seed(0)
ref=inp.Model(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to(device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
torch.manual_seed(0)
mod=out.ModelNew(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to(device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
mod.load_state_dict(ref.state_dict())
x=inp.get_inputs()[0].to('cuda')
with torch.no_grad():
    y_ref=ref(x)
    y=mod(x)
    d=(y.float()-y_ref.float()).abs()
    print('final max', d.max().item(), 'mean', d.mean().item())
    x_contig=x.contiguous(); mod._refresh_static_buffers(x_contig.device, x_contig.dtype)
    a_pack=out._pack_a(x_contig)
    out.gemm_mfma_kernel[out._launch_gemm](a_pack.view(-1), mod._b_pack.view(-1), mod._bias, mod._y)
    y_gemm=mod._y.clone(); y_ref_gemm=ref.gemm(x)
    dg=(y_gemm.float()-y_ref_gemm.float()).abs()
    print('gemm max', dg.max().item(), 'mean', dg.mean().item())
PY" in /workspace/kernel_benchmark

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

I’m using the existing kernel as a black box now and sweeping a tiny set of plausible `A`/`B` pack layouts offline. That’s faster than editing the file repeatedly, and it should tell me which swizzle the kernel actually expects.

/bin/bash -lc "python - <<'PY'
import importlib.util, torch
round_dir='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds/round2'

def load(path,name):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name,path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod
inp=load(f'{round_dir}/input_model.py','inp')
out=load(f'{round_dir}/output_model_new.py','out')

BATCH=out.BATCH_SIZE; IN=out.IN_FEATURES; OUT=out.OUT_FEATURES; WM=out.WARP_M; WN=out.WARP_N; KT=out.K_TILE

def pack_a_cand(x):
    xb=x.view(BATCH//WM, WM, IN//KT, KT).permute(0,2,1,3)
    return torch.cat((xb[:,:,:,0:8], xb[:,:,:,8:16]), dim=2).contiguous()

def pack_a_patch(x):
    xb=x.view(BATCH//WM, WM, IN//KT, KT).permute(0,2,1,3)
    first=torch.cat((xb[:,:,:,0:4], xb[:,:,:,8:12]), dim=-1)
    second=torch.cat((xb[:,:,:,4:8], xb[:,:,:,12:16]), dim=-1)
    return torch.cat((first, second), dim=2).contiguous()

def pack_b_cand(w):
    wb=w.view(IN//KT, KT, OUT//WN, WN).permute(0,2,1,3)
    groups=[]
    for g in range(WN//4):
        cols=wb[:,:,:,g*4:(g+1)*4]
        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:,:,0:8,:], cols[:,:,8:16,:]), dim=-1))
    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()

def pack_b_alt(w):
    wb=w.view(IN//KT, KT, OUT//WN, WN).permute(0,2,1,3)  # [ktile, ntile, k, col]
    # lane order by k first then 4-col group
    lanes=[]
    for k in range(8):
        row=[]
        for g in range(WN//4):
            cols=wb[:,:,k,g*4:(g+1)*4]
            cols2=wb[:,:,k+8,g*4:(g+1)*4]
            row.append(torch.cat((cols, cols2), dim=-1).unsqueeze(2))
        lanes.append(torch.cat(row, dim=2))
    return torch.cat(lanes, dim=2).contiguous()

packs_a=[('a_cand',pack_a_cand),('a_patch',pack_a_patch)]
packs_b=[('b_cand',pack_b_cand),('b_alt',pack_b_alt)]

torch.manual_seed(0)
ref=inp.Model(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to(device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
x=inp.get_inputs()[0].to('cuda')
y_ref=ref.gemm(x)
for an,af in packs_a:
  for bn,bf in packs_b:
    torch.cuda.empty_cache()
    y=torch.empty((BATCH,OUT), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    a=af(x).view(-1)
    b=bf(ref.gemm.weight.t().contiguous()).view(-1)
    bias=ref.gemm.bias.contiguous()
    out.gemm_mfma_kernel[out._launch_gemm](a,b,bias,y)
    d=(y.float()-y_ref.float()).abs()
    print(an,bn,'max',d.max().item(),'mean',d.mean().item())

import importlib.util, torch
round_dir='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p30/optimization_rounds/round2'

def load(path,name):
    spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(name,path)
    mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
    spec.loader.exec_module(mod)
    return mod
inp=load(f'{round_dir}/input_model.py','inp')
out=load(f'{round_dir}/output_model_new.py','out')
BATCH=out.BATCH_SIZE; IN=out.IN_FEATURES; OUT=out.OUT_FEATURES; WM=out.WARP_M; WN=out.WARP_N; KT=out.K_TILE

def pack_a(x):
    xb=x.view(BATCH//WM, WM, IN//KT, KT).permute(0,2,1,3)
    return torch.cat((xb[:,:,:,0:8], xb[:,:,:,8:16]), dim=2).contiguous()

def pack_b_cand(w):
    wb=w.view(IN//KT, KT, OUT//WN, WN).permute(0,2,1,3)
    groups=[]
    for g in range(WN//4):
        cols=wb[:,:,:,g*4:(g+1)*4]
        groups.append(torch.cat((cols[:,:,0:8,:], cols[:,:,8:16,:]), dim=-1))
    return torch.cat(groups, dim=2).contiguous()

torch.manual_seed(0)
ref=inp.Model(*inp.get_init_inputs()).to(device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
x=inp.get_inputs()[0].to('cuda')
y_ref=ref.gemm(x)
a=pack_a(x).view(-1)
for name,w in [('wt', ref.gemm.weight.t().contiguous()), ('w', ref.gemm.weight.contiguous())]:
    y=torch.empty((BATCH,OUT), device='cuda', dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    b=pack_b_cand(w).view(-1)
    out.gemm_mfma_kernel[out._launch_gemm](a,b,ref.gemm.bias.contiguous(),y)
    d=(y.float()-y_ref.float()).abs()
    print(name,'max',d.max().item(),'mean',d.mean().item())

def _launch_gemm():
    return ((OUT_FEATURES // BLOCK_N, BATCH_SIZE // BLOCK_M, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))


def _launch_post():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_kernel(
    a_pack: S.Tensor((A_PACK_ELEMS,), S.bf16),
    b_pack: S.Tensor((B_PACK_ELEMS,), S.bf16),
    bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid % WARP_SIZE
    warp = tid // WARP_SIZE
    warp_row = warp // 2
    warp_col = warp % 2

    block_row = S.block_id(1) * BLOCK_M
    block_col = S.block_id(0) * BLOCK_N
    tile_row = block_row + warp_row * WARP_M
    tile_col = block_col + warp_col * WARP_N

    a_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(a_pack, A_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)
    b_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(b_pack, B_PACK_RANGE_BYTES)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    acc = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    a_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)
    b_smem = S.make_shared((NUM_WARPS, WARP_SIZE, 8), S.bf16)

    for k_tile in S.range(A_PACK_K):
        a_elem_offset = (((tile_row // WARP_M) * A_PACK_K + k_tile) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        b_elem_offset = ((k_tile * B_PACK_N + (tile_col // WARP_N)) * WARP_SIZE + lane) * 8
        a_byte_offset = S.convert(a_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)
        b_byte_offset = S.convert(b_elem_offset * 2, S.i32)

        a_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(a_rsrc, zero, a_byte_offset, 0)
        b_frag_g = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(b_rsrc, zero, b_byte_offset, 0)

        a_frag_view = S.view(a_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag_view = S.view(b_frag_g, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

        for frag_half in S.range(2):
            for frag_elem in S.range(4):
                a_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = a_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]
                b_smem[warp, lane, frag_half * 4 + frag_elem] = b_frag_view[frag_half, frag_elem, 0]

        S.syncthreads()

        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[0], b_frag_view[0], acc)
        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag_view[1], b_frag_view[1], acc)

        S.syncthreads()

    lane_col = lane % 32
    lane_row_quad = lane // 32
    for acc_idx in S.range(16):
        out_col = tile_col + lane_col
        out_row = tile_row + 8 * (acc_idx // 4) + 4 * lane_row_quad + (acc_idx % 4)
        value = acc[acc_idx] + S.convert(bias[out_col], S.f32)
        y[out_row, out_col] = S.convert(value, S.bf16)


@substrate.jit
def groupnorm_hardtanh_kernel(
    y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, OUT_FEATURES), S.bf16),
    gn_weight: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
    gn_bias: S.Tensor((OUT_FEATURES,), S.f32),
):
    for row in S.range(BATCH_SIZE):
        for group in S.range(NUM_GROUPS):
            mean = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                mean += S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32)
            mean = mean / S.convert(GROUP_SIZE, S.f32)
            var = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
            for t in S.range(GROUP_SIZE):
                c = group * GROUP_SIZE + t
                diff = S.convert(y[row, c], S.f32) - mean
